< Text>
A Relaxing and tranquil place to go and enjoy the day.  The  park is beautifully kept up with clean facilities, as well as BBQ pits, horseshoe pit's, picnic tables two farely large group area's and small playground for the kids.. And an extra added perk to it is it's walking distance from the Chumash Casino.<//Text>

<Time>1601439958227< /Time><user_id>102964145193075165937</user_id>< text>
This was a nice little park in Santa Ynez with lots of benches and shade. There is a children's playground, BBQ grills, covered group picnic tables and bathrooms. DOGS ARE ALLOWED ON A LEASH. The park host, Marta, waved and came to say "Hello." She is the nicest person and gave us the best tips on where to eat in town. She really takes good care of the park, keeping it nice and green all year round for people to enjoy.

Google Maps directions to the park are incorrect. From Edison St., turn onto Numancia St. to get to the parking lot.< /text>

< review>
My wife and I recently purchased a 2017 29' Forest River Salem Cruise Lite.
Our experience at Major RV was beyond easy.  Eric was our salesperson. He was patient and answered all our questions to our satisfaction.  There was absolutely no pressure.  The no haggle price was still cheaper than other dealers and they don't charge a pre-delivery inspection fee.  There was no hidden fees added either.  Jeremy and Eric made sure we didn't buy more trailer than our tow vehicle can handle.  It's no secret that some dealers will sell you a 10,000 LB trailer and tell you your Fiat will tow it fine.  We used our own financing but Melissa in the finance department was very nice and tried her best to beat our pre-qualified rate.  The pre-delivery inspection was thorough and easy.  Final paperwork was a breeze. They even delivered the trailer to our home because we hadn't gotten around to installing our hitch (we live local).   We will definitely be back when it's time to upgrade.
Be sure and ask for Eric.< /review>

< Review>
Bought a new 2014 Salem Cruise Lite travel trailer.  Anthony was my sales person and was patient with me throughout the entirety of the sale.  Their prices were the lowest around so they didn't really negotiate on price (just a couple hundred) and I scoured the trailer before taking delivery and found a few minor issues which they addressed immediately.  I mean, I really checked everything using a checklist I found online.  He didn't rush me during the PDI and walked me through the trailer showing me how everything works, which is standard practice, but was nice anyway.  They also set up my weight distribution equipment on the trailer while I was inspecting the trailer.  I passed on their aftermarket warranty and recommend instead getting the 2nd year warranty direct from Forest River for $150 (or $250 depending on model).

I did end up having an issue with the floor during the first outing and the service department was spot on coordinating the repair with Forest River in Rialto and I got my trailer back in no time.  I was upset that the linoleum floor needed to be replaced, but that wasn't the dealer's fault and they were great with the warranty coverage.  The lesson here is to check the floor with your BARE FEET, not just shoes. ;)

It's a small RV dealer and overall a first class operation, I recommend.< /Review>
